\draw[black] [shift={(-2.5,2.5)}] (2pt,0) -- (-2pt,0) node[left]{ \scriptsize{\num[round-mode=places,round-precision=2]{2.5}}};
\end{scope}
\begin{scope}[yshift=0cm]
\draw[black] [shift={(-2.5,-2.5)}] (0,2pt) -- (0,-2pt) node[below]{ \scriptsize{\num[round-mode=places,round-precision=2]{-2.5}}};
\draw[black] [shift={(-2.0,-2.5)}] (0,2pt) -- (0,-2pt) node[below]{ \scriptsize{\num[round-mode=places,round-precision=2]{-2.0}}};
\draw[black] [shift={(-1.5,-2.5)}] (0,2pt) -- (0,-2pt) node[below]{ \scriptsize{\num[round-mode=places,round-precision=2]{-1.5}}};
\draw[black] [shift={(-1.0,-2.5)}] (0,2pt) -- (0,-2pt) node[below]{ \scriptsize{\num[round-mode=places,round-precision=2]{-1.0}}};
\draw[black] [shift={(-0.5,-2.5)}] (0,2pt) -- (0,-2pt) node[below]{ \scriptsize{\num[round-mode=places,round-precision=2]{-0.5}}};
\draw[black] [shift={(0.0,-2.5)}] (0,2pt) -- (0,-2pt) node[below]{ \scriptsize{\num[round-mode=places,round-precision=2]{0.0}}};
\draw[black] [shift={(0.5,-2.5)}] (0,2pt) -- (0,-2pt) node[below]{ \scriptsize{\num[round-mode=places,round-precision=2]{0.5}}};
\draw[black] [shift={(1.0,-2.5)}] (0,2pt) -- (0,-2pt) node[below]{ \scriptsize{\num[round-mode=places,round-precision=2]{1.0}}};
\draw[black] [shift={(1.5,-2.5)}] (0,2pt) -- (0,-2pt) node[below]{ \scriptsize{\num[round-mode=places,round-precision=2]{1.5}}};
\draw[black] [shift={(2.0,-2.5)}] (0,2pt) -- (0,-2pt) node[below]{ \scriptsize{\num[round-mode=places,round-precision=2]{2.0}}};
\draw[black] [shift={(2.5,-2.5)}] (0,2pt) -- (0,-2pt) node[below]{ \scriptsize{\num[round-mode=places,round-precision=2]{2.5}}};
\end{scope}
\end{scope}
\pgfsetxvec{\pgfpoint{1cm}{0cm}}
\pgfsetyvec{\pgfpoint{0cm}{1cm}}
\end{scope}
\end{tikzpicture}
